<h1 style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><u><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="font-size:14.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></u></b></font></h1>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font style="border:none;"><font face=Courier lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; &nbsp;</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; John R. Howe</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Executive Vice President</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Chief Financial Officer</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 704-551-7315</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></font></p>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.5pt;padding:31.0pt 31.0pt 1.0pt 31.0pt;">

<p align=center style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;padding:0in;text-align:center;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:14.0pt;">CATO REPORTS 4Q AND FULL-YEAR EARNINGS</font></b></font></p>

</div>


<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:-.15pt;line-height:150%;">&nbsp;</font></font></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">CHARLOTTE, N.C. (March 19,
2020) &#8211;&#8211; </font></font><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">The&nbsp;Cato Corporation&nbsp;(NYSE: CATO) today
reported earnings for the fourth quarter and year ended&nbsp;February 1,
2020.&nbsp; For the fourth quarter, the Company reported a net loss
of&nbsp;$3.2 million, or a loss of&nbsp;$0.13&nbsp;per diluted share, compared
to a net loss of&nbsp;$3.2 million&nbsp;or&nbsp;a loss of $0.13&nbsp;per
diluted share for the prior fourth quarter ended&nbsp;February 2, 2019.&nbsp;
Full-year fiscal 2019 net income was&nbsp;$35.9
million&nbsp;or&nbsp;$1.46&nbsp;per diluted share compared to&nbsp;$30.5
million&nbsp;or&nbsp;$1.23&nbsp;per diluted share for 2018.&nbsp; For the year,
net income increased 18% and earnings per diluted share increased 19% from the
prior year.&nbsp;</font></font></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">Sales for fiscal fourth quarter ended&nbsp;February 1,
2020&nbsp;were&nbsp;$188.4 million, a decrease of 1% from sales of&nbsp;$190.3
million&nbsp;for the fourth quarter ended&nbsp;February 2, 2019.&nbsp; For the
quarter, same-store sales increased 1% from last year. &#160;For the year, the
Company's sales decreased 1% to&nbsp;$816.2 million&nbsp;from 2018 sales
of&nbsp;$821.1 million.&nbsp; Same-store sales for the year increased 2% to
last year.&#160;&#160;&#160; &#160;&#160;&#160;</font></font></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">&quot;We are encouraged by the growth experienced in 2019,
building off a stabilized 2018,&#8221; said John Cato, Chairman, President and Chief
Executive Officer.&nbsp;&#8220;We continued to focus on our product and merchandise
assortments, while maintaining strong inventory control.&#8221; </font></font></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">Fourth-quarter gross margin increased to 34.3% of sales from 33.1%
of sales in 2018 due primarily to improved merchandise margins partially offset
by higher occupancy costs.&nbsp; Selling, general and administrative expenses
were 35.6% of sales, compared to 34.7% in the prior year.&nbsp; SG&amp;A costs
as a percent of sales were higher primarily due to higher incentive
compensation partially offset by lower </font></font><!-- Do not modify beyond this point! !--><a name=bcl_connect_next></a></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><a name=bcl_connect_prev></a><!-- Do not modify before this point! !--><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">store impairment
charges. Income tax for the quarter was an expense of $0.8 million compared to
a benefit of $0.3 million last year.&#160; The tax expense is primarily due to
discrete items that were recognized during the fourth quarter of 2019.&#160; </font></font></p>

<p align=left style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:left;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:0pt;line-height:150%;">For 2019,
gross margin increased to 37.6% of sales from 36.4% of sales in 2018 due to
increased merchandise margins.&nbsp; Selling, general and administrative
expenses increased to 32.3%&nbsp;of sales compared to 31.9% in the prior
year.&nbsp; The selling, general and administrative expense increase was
primarily due to increased incentive compensation partially offset by lower
store impairment charges and insurance costs.&#160; Income tax for the year was an
expense of $7.3 million compared to an expense of $2.6 million last year.&#160; </font></font></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">&quot;Cato continues to maintain a strong balance sheet, with
approximately&nbsp;$212 million&nbsp;in unrestricted cash and short-term
investments and no debt,&quot; Mr. Cato said.&nbsp; &#8220;As a company, our priority
remains to provide great value to our customers, opportunity for growth to our
associates, and strong returns to our shareholders.&#8221; During 2019, the Company
returned&nbsp;$42.2 million&nbsp;to shareholders through dividends of&nbsp;$32.6
million&nbsp;and share repurchases of&nbsp;$9.6 million.&nbsp; The Company
maintained its quarterly dividend of&nbsp;$0.33&nbsp;per share,
or&nbsp;$1.32&nbsp;over the year. &nbsp;For the fiscal year ended&nbsp;February
1, 2020, the Company opened 5 stores and closed 35 stores.&nbsp; As
of&nbsp;February 1, 2020, the Company operated 1,281 stores in 31 states.&nbsp;</font></font></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">We continue to assess the potential impact of the coronavirus,
which remains uncertain at this time.&#160; Because of the uncertainties we are not
providing a 2020 outlook or assumptions.&nbsp; There remains a high level of
uncertainty over the extent of supply chain disruption, and as many other
retailers, we are seeing the dramatic impact on our customers and are unsure
how long this will continue.</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font color=#333333 face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">We are
monitoring this unprecedented situation and continue to be mindful of the
current events unfolding and of the safety of our customers and associates.&#160;
And although we cannot quantify the impact of this unprecedented situation,
first quarter results will be negatively impacted.</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman,serif" style="border:none;"><b><font face="Times New Roman,serif" lang=EN-US style="font-size:11.0pt;">THE CATO CORPORATION</font></b></font></p>

<h3 style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font face="Times New Roman,serif" style="border:none;"><b><font face="Times New Roman,serif" style="font-size:11.0pt;">CONDENSED
CONSOLIDATED STA<a name=IS></a><a name="IS_bclEnd"></a>TEMENTS OF INCOME
(UNAUDITED)</font></b></font></h3>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman,serif" style="border:none;"><b><font face="Times New Roman,serif" lang=EN-US style="font-size:11.0pt;">FOR THE PERIODS ENDED FEBRUARY
1, 2020 AND FEBRUARY 2, 2019</font></b></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman,serif" style="border:none;"><font face="Times New Roman,serif" lang=EN-US style="font-size:9.0pt;">(Dollars in thousands, except per share
data)</font></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face="Times New Roman,serif" lang=EN-US style="font-size:11.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
